	CHI_spy_family_NBIS_recharge = {

		allowed = {
			tag = CHI
		}
		fire_only_once = yes
		available = {
			agency_upgrade_number > 6
		}
		visible = {
			tag = CHI
			
		}
		complete_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = NBIS_spy_family
				add_idea = NBIS_spy_family_guy
			}
		}
	}
	CHI_restore_power_to_clean_up_G4_robber = {
		icon = generic_wall_line
		allowed = {
			tag = CHI
		}

			has_political_power  > 1000
			surrender_progress > 0.6
		}

	PRC_support_mao_clique = {	#积累毛泽东支持

		icon = eng_propaganda_campaigns
		allowed = {
			tag = PRC
		} 
		available = {
			OR = {
				has_idea_with_trait = maoists_trait_zhang_wentian
				has_idea_with_trait = maoists_trait_mao_zedong
				has_idea_with_trait = maoists_trait_chen_yun

			}
		}

		priority = 1000
		#cost = 120
		custom_cost_trigger = {
			political_power_growth > 0.75
		}
		custom_cost_text = pp_per_day_neg_075
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { 
								parliament_seat_array^1 < parliament_seat_array^0 
							}
							check_variable = { 
								parliament_seat_array^1 < parliament_seat_array^2 
							}
							check_variable = { 
								parliament_seat_array^1 < parliament_seat_array^3

							}

								character = PRC_lin_boqu
								ruling_only = yes
							}
							has_country_leader = { 
								character = PRC_zhang_wentian 
								ruling_only = yes 
							}
						}
					}
				}
			 }
		}
		days_remove = 90
		modifier = {
			political_power_gain = -0.75
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			random_list = {
				15 = {
					set_temp_variable = { 
						temp_member = 2 
					}
					set_temp_variable = { 
						temp_seats = 0.05

					}
					modify_parliament_seat = yes
				}
				20 = {
					set_temp_variable = {

					modify_parliament_seat = yes

					}

					modify_parliament_seat = yes

			}
		}
		activation = {
			always = no 
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
		timeout_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = RCM_comchina_decisions.7
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				count_wang_ming = 1
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { count_wang_ming < 4 }
				}
				add_days_mission_timeout  = {
					mission = RCM_wang_ming_demand_meeting_mission
					days = -30
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { 
				temp_member = 3

				limit = { 
					leader_is_maoist = yes 
				}

					temp_member = 2 
				}
				set_temp_variable = { 
					temp_seats = -0.05

							has_country_leader = { 
								character = prc_wang_ming 
								ruling_only = yes	
							}
						}
					}    

					AND = {
							OR = {
							check_variable = { 
								parliament_seat_array^3 < parliament_seat_array^0 
							}
							check_variable = { 
								parliament_seat_array^3 < parliament_seat_array^1 
							}
							check_variable = { 
								parliament_seat_array^3 < parliament_seat_array^2 
							}
						}
						OR = {

							has_country_leader = { 
								character = PRC_chen_duxiu ruling_only = yes	
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

			always = no
		}
		fixed_random_seed = no
		timeout_effect = { 
			country_event = {
				id = RCM_comchina_decisions.2
			}
			effect_tooltip = {		
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_stability < 0.15
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							AND = {
								OR = {
									check_variable = { 
										parliament_seat_array^0 < parliament_seat_array^1 
									}
									check_variable = { 
										parliament_seat_array^0 < parliament_seat_array^2

						}
					}

						limit = {
							AND = {
								OR = {
									check_variable = { 
										parliament_seat_array^1 < parliament_seat_array^0 
									}

										parliament_seat_array^1 < parliament_seat_array^2 
									}

									}
								}

									}

										character = PRC_lin_boqu
										ruling_only = yes
									}
									has_country_leader = { 
										character = PRC_zhang_wentian 
										ruling_only = yes 
									}
								}
							}
						}
						country_event = {
							id = RCM_comchina_decisions.4
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							AND = {
								OR = {
									check_variable = { 
										parliament_seat_array^2 < parliament_seat_array^0 
									}
									check_variable = { 
										parliament_seat_array^2 < parliament_seat_array^1

										parliament_seat_array^2 < parliament_seat_array^3 
									}

									}

										ruling_only = yes	
									}
								}
							}    
						}
						country_event = {
							id = RCM_comchina_decisions.5
						}
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							AND = {
								OR = {

									}
									check_variable = {

PRC_move_capital_cat = {	#转移中央机关驻地
	PRC_move_capital_decision = { 
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_form_nation
		allowed = {
			is_literally_china = yes
		}
		
		state_target = yes
		
		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_capital = no 
				is_in_home_area = yes
			}
		}


		visible = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_completed_focus = PRC_Guerrilla_warfare_orientation
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = PRC_A_New_Country
					has_completed_focus = PRC_For_the_Soviets
					has_completed_focus = PRC_Federal_Republic
				}
			}
		}
		available = {
			FROM = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_capital = no 
				is_in_home_area = yes
			}
			has_war = yes
		}

		cost = 25
		days_remove = 30

            political_power_gain = -0.25
		}

			base = 0

						region = 143

						region = 242
					}
				}
				any_owned_state = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_capital = yes
					is_in_home_area = yes
					region = 245
				}
				count_triggers = {
					amount > 4
					controls_state = 715

		            controls_state = 1153
		            controls_state = 328

@offsive_days = 30
PRC_civil_war_offensives = {	#内战攻势

	PRC_northern_man_offensive = {	#北满

		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans

		allowed = {
			tag = PRC
		}

		available = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_242
					region = 242
				}
				controller = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			NOT = { 
				has_active_mission = prc_preparing_offensive 
			}
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_242
					region = 242
				}
				OR = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					num_owned_neighbour_states = {
						owner = ROOT
						count > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		cost = 0

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = @offsive_days

		visible = {
			tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
			has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader

			has_global_flag = CHI_no_longer_united_flag
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_242
					region = 242
				}
			}
			NOT = {
                has_active_mission = prc_northern_man_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			activate_mission = prc_northern_man_offensive_mission
			set_country_flag = prc_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
					NOT = {
						tag = PRC
					}
				}
				activate_mission = prc_northern_man_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.big_china
				if = {
					limit = {
						region = 242
					}
					clr_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
					remove_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive
					}
				}
			}
			
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					all_of_scopes = {
						array = global.big_china
						has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
						region = 242
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT	
					}
					NOT = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = global.big_china
							has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
							region = 242
							controller = {
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}   
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 200
				tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
			}
		}
	}

					remove_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive
					}
				}
			}
			
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					all_of_scopes = {
						array = global.big_china
						has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
						region = 155
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT	
					}
					NOT = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = global.big_china
							has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
							region = 155
							controller = {
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
						}

    prc_north_china_offensive = {	#华北

		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans

		allowed = {
			tag = PRC
		}

		available = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_143
					region = 143
				}
				controller = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			NOT = { 
				has_active_mission = prc_preparing_offensive 
			}
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_143
					region = 143
				}
				OR = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					num_owned_neighbour_states = {
						owner = ROOT
						count > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = { 
				region = 143
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
			}

 			highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		cost = 0

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = @offsive_days

		visible = {
			tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
			has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			has_global_flag = CHI_no_longer_united_flag
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_143
					region = 143
				}
			}
			NOT = {
                has_active_mission = prc_north_china_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			activate_mission = prc_preparing_offensive
			set_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
						tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					}
				}
				activate_mission = prc_north_china_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.big_china
				if = {
					limit = {
						region = 143
					}
					clr_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
					remove_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					all_of_scopes = {
						array = global.big_china
						has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
						region = 143
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT	
					}
					NOT = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = global.big_china
							has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
							region = 143
							controller = {
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}  
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 180
				tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
			}
		}
	}

					remove_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					all_of_scopes = {
						array = global.big_china
						has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
						region = 246
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT	
					}
					NOT = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = global.big_china
							has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
							region = 246
							controller = {
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}  
			}
		}

	prc_east_china_offensive = {	#华东

		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans

		allowed = {
			tag = PRC
		}

		available = {

					region = 247
				}
				controller = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}

				has_active_mission = prc_preparing_offensive 
			}
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_247
					region = 247
				}
				OR = {
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
					num_owned_neighbour_states = {
						owner = ROOT
						count > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = { 
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				region = 247
			}

 			highlight_color_before_active = 3
			highlight_color_while_active = 2
		}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		cost = 0

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_remove = @offsive_days

		visible = {
			tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
			has_war_with = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
			has_global_flag = CHI_no_longer_united_flag
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.big_china
				tooltip = big_china_tt
				has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = is_in_strat_247
					region = 247
				}
			}
			NOT = {
                has_active_mission = prc_east_china_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			activate_mission = prc_preparing_offensive
			set_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = event_target:WTT_current_china_leader
						tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
					}
				}
				activate_mission = prc_east_china_offensive_mission
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.big_china
				if = {
					limit = {
						region = 247
					}
					clr_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
					remove_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = prc_unplanned_offensive
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 0.1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					all_of_scopes = {
						array = global.big_china
						has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
						region = 247
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT	
					}
					NOT = {
						any_of_scopes = {
							array = global.big_china
							has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
							region = 247
							controller = {
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
						}
					}
				}  
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				any_of_scopes = {
					array = global.big_china
					has_state_flag = chi_unplanned_offensive_flag
					region = 247
					controller = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
					num_owned_neighbour_states = {
						owner = ROOT
						count > 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	prc_preparing_offensive = {		#准备攻势

		icon = hol_draw_up_staff_plans

		allowed = {
			tag = PRC
		}

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { 
				always = no 
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_mission_timeout = @offsive_days

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			hidden_trigger = {
                OR = {
					tag = event_target:WTT_communist_china
				}
			}
			has_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = chi_preparing_offensive_in_progress_flag
		}
	}

 	chi_northern_man_offensive_mission = {		#北满

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = PRC_liaoshen_campaign
			tag = PRC
			716 = {
				num_owned_neighbour_states = {
					owner = ROOT
					count > 0
				}

				controller = {
					has_war_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.big_china
				if = {
					limit = {
						region = 155
					}

					add_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = PRC_regional_offensive
					}
				}
			}
		}

		days_remove = 90

		remove_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.big_china
				if = {
					limit = {
						region = 155
						has_dynamic_modifier = {
							modifier = PRC_regional_offensive
						}
					}

					remove_dynamic_modifier = {
						modifier = PRC_regional_offensive
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
